# Boards Manual
## Your Project Execution Workspace

---

## OUTLINE STRUCTURE

## CHAPTER 1: INTRODUCTION TO BOARDS

Transform strategic workflows into tactical execution spaces.

### 1.1 What is a Board?

**Definition:**

A **board** is your Kanban-style project execution workspace where high-level compliance workflows transform into actionable, trackable tasks. While workflows define *what* needs to be done, boards are *where* you actually do it.

**Kanban-Style Project Management:**

```
Kanban Principles Applied:
- Visualize work (columns show task states)
- Limit work in progress (WIP limits)
- Manage flow (cards move left to right)
- Make process explicit (clear stages)
- Continuous improvement (metrics and tracking)
```

**Visual Example:**

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
```

**Micro-Level Execution Space:**

```
Templates â†’ Workflows â†’ Boards

Templates: Define structure
  \"ISO 27001 has 93 controls across 4 domains\"

Workflows: Map requirements
  \"Each control needs a policy, implementation, and evidence\"

Boards: Execute tasks
  \"Create MFA policy (Due: Friday, Assigned: John)\"
```

**Where Workflows Become Action:**

```
Workflow Unit (Macro):
â–¼ A.9.4.3 Multi-Factor Authentication
  Description: Implement MFA for all admin accounts...
  Tags: [Critical] [IT] [Q1-2024]

Transforms Into Board Tasks (Micro):
â”œâ”€ Task 1: Research MFA solutions (Due: Jan 5, Assigned: Sarah)
â”œâ”€ Task 2: Get budget approval (Due: Jan 10, Assigned: CFO)
â”œâ”€ Task 3: Purchase Duo licenses (Due: Jan 15, Assigned: IT Manager)
â”œâ”€ Task 4: Configure Duo for admins (Due: Jan 20, Assigned: John)
â””â”€ Task 5: Train admin users (Due: Jan 25, Assigned: Sarah)

One workflow item = Multiple executable tasks
```

**Task Tracking and Collaboration:**

```
Board Features:
âœ“ Assign tasks to team members
âœ“ Set due dates and reminders
âœ“ Track task progress through columns
âœ“ Add checklists within tasks
âœ“ Attach files and links
âœ“ Comment and collaborate
âœ“ Organize with milestones and categories
âœ“ Group related tasks
âœ“ View team workload
```

### 1.2 Boards in Compliance Execution

**The Three-Tier Execution Model:**

```
Tier 1: Templates (Structure)
  \"What fields and levels exist?\"
  
Tier 2: Workflows (Strategy)
  \"What compliance requirements must we meet?\"
  
Tier 3: Boards (Tactics) â† WE ARE HERE
  \"How do we actually implement these requirements?\"
```

**Workflow Blueprints â†’ Execution Tasks:**

```
Consultant Creates Workflow:
\"GDPR Article 32: Security of Processing\"
â”œâ”€ Implement encryption
â”œâ”€ Implement access controls
â”œâ”€ Implement logging
â””â”€ Conduct regular audits

Exports to Board â†“

Client Creates Execution Tasks:
â”‚
â”œâ”€ Encryption:
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Task: Evaluate encryption solutions
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Task: Purchase encryption tool
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Task: Deploy encryption on database
â”‚  â””â”€ Task: Test encryption verification
â”‚
â”œâ”€ Access Controls:
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Task: Document access control policy
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Task: Implement MFA
â”‚  â””â”€ Task: Conduct access review
â”‚
â””â”€ ... (more tasks)

Blueprint shows WHAT
Board shows WHO, WHEN, HOW
```

**Consultant References â†’ Client Workspace:**

```
Two-Panel Interface:

Consultant: Controls compliance framework
Client: Controls execution plan
```

**Strategic Map â†’ Tactical Operations:**

```
Workflow (Strategic):
\"Implement ISO 27001 across organization\"
- 93 controls
- 12-month timeline
- Multiple departments

Board (Tactical):
Sprint 1 (Jan-Feb):
- 15 tasks
- IT department focus
- Critical controls first

Sprint 2 (Mar-Apr):
- 20 tasks
- HR and Finance
- Medium priority controls

Etc...

Strategy: What we need to achieve (big picture)
Tactics: How we achieve it (day-to-day actions)
```

**Compliance Requirements â†’ Implementation Tasks:**

```
Requirement (from workflow):
\"GDPR Article 5(1)(f): Integrity and Confidentiality\"
\"Personal data shall be processed in a manner that ensures 
appropriate security... including protection against 
unauthorized or unlawful processing.\"

Implementation Tasks (on board):
â”œâ”€ Task: Conduct data inventory
â”‚  Assigned: Data Protection Officer
â”‚  Due: Week 1
â”‚  Milestone: Phase 1 - Assessment
â”‚
â”œâ”€ Task: Classify data sensitivity
â”‚  Assigned: IT Security Team
â”‚  Due: Week 2
â”‚  Milestone: Phase 1 - Assessment
â”‚
â”œâ”€ Task: Implement encryption at rest
â”‚  Assigned: Database Admin
â”‚  Due: Week 4
â”‚  Milestone: Phase 2 - Implementation
â”‚
â””â”€ ... (more tasks)

Abstract requirement â†’ Concrete, assignable, due-dated tasks
```

**Use Case Example:**

```
Scenario: Acme Corp needs GDPR compliance

Step 1: Consultant creates GDPR workflow
- Maps all GDPR requirements
- Adds descriptions and guidance
- Tags by priority and department

Step 2: Export workflow to board
- Creates \"Acme Corp GDPR Compliance\" board
- Workflow appears in References panel (locked)
- Main board area is empty (ready for tasks)

Step 3: Client creates implementation plan
- Reviews requirement in References
- Creates specific tasks in To Do column
- Assigns to team members
- Sets due dates and milestones
- Tracks progress through columns

Step 4: Execution
- Team works on tasks
- Moves tasks through columns
- Consultant monitors references
- Client manages execution
- Progress visible to both parties

Result:
- Clear separation of concerns
- Consultant expertise preserved
- Client autonomy maintained
- Compliance achieved through structured execution
```

---

### 1.3 Board Components Overview

**The Seven Core Components:**

Boards are built from 7 interconnected components that work together to create a complete project management experience.

---

**1. Columns (Workflow States):**

```
Purpose: Represent stages of work

Default Columns:
To Do â†’ In Progress â†’ Review â†’ Done

Customizable:
You can add, rename, reorder, or delete columns to match your workflow

Example Custom Columns:
Backlog â†’ To Do â†’ In Progress â†’ Code Review â†’ QA Testing â†’ Deployed

Each column = A state your task can be in
```

**2. Cards (Tasks):**

```
Purpose: Individual work items

Card Properties:
- Title and description
- Assigned team members
- Due dates and start dates
- Checklists (sub-tasks)
- Attachments (files, links)
- Comments and activity log
- Tags and labels
- Progress indicators

One card = One task/deliverable
```

**3. Dynamic Lists (Reference Trees):**

```
Purpose: Collapsible reference structures (from exported workflows)

Features:
- Tree/hierarchy display
- Expand/collapse sections
- Search and filter
- Read-only (consultant controlled)
- Link cards to reference items

Use Case: Compliance frameworks, requirement libraries, documentation trees
```

**4. Milestones (Time Phases):**

```
Purpose: Group tasks by time-based phases

Examples:
- Sprint 1 (Jan 1-15)
- Q1 Objectives
- Phase 1: Planning
- MVP Release

Features:
- Link multiple cards to milestone
- Auto-track completion %
- Visual progress indicators
- Filter board by milestone
```

**5. Categories (Organizational Buckets):**

```
Purpose: Classify cards by type/theme

Examples:
- Documentation
- Development
- Testing
- Deployment

Features:
- Color-coded
- Icon-based
- Filter board by category
- Count cards per category
```

**6. Groups (Task Collections):**

```
Purpose: Create logical groupings of related cards

Examples:
- \"MFA Implementation\" group (5 related tasks)
- \"Q1 Security Controls\" group (12 controls)
- \"Vendor Assessments\" group (8 vendors)

Features:
- Multi-card collections
- Group-level progress tracking
- Visual grouping on board
- Bulk operations
```

**7. Members (Team Collaboration):**

```
Purpose: Team member management

Features:
- Add/remove team members
- Assign roles (admin, member, viewer)
- Avatar display
- @mentions in comments
- Assignment tracking
- Workload visibility
```

**How Components Work Together:**

```
Example Board:

Milestone: \"Sprint 1 - Critical Controls\"
â”œâ”€ Category: Technical Controls
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Group: MFA Implementation
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Card: Research MFA solutions (To Do, Assigned: Sarah)
â”‚  â”‚  â”œâ”€ Card: Purchase licenses (To Do, Assigned: IT Manager)
â”‚  â”‚  â””â”€ Card: Deploy MFA (In Progress, Assigned: John)
â”‚  â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€ Group: Encryption
â”‚     â”œâ”€ Card: Evaluate encryption tools (Review, Assigned: DBA)
â”‚     â””â”€ Card: Deploy encryption (Done, Assigned: DBA)
â”‚
â””â”€ Category: Administrative Controls
   â””â”€ Card: Draft InfoSec Policy (Done, Assigned: Legal)

All cards in columns (To Do, In Progress, Review, Done)
Cards have categories (Technical, Administrative)
Cards grouped logically (MFA, Encryption)
All linked to Milestone (Sprint 1)
All assigned to team Members
```

**Component Interactions:**

```
Dynamic List (Reference) â†â†’ Cards (Tasks)
  \"Link card to requirement\"
  Track which requirement a task addresses

Milestone (Phase) â†â†’ Cards (Tasks)
  \"Add card to milestone\"
  Track phase completion

Category (Type) â†â†’ Cards (Tasks)
  \"Categorize card\"
  Filter board by category

Group (Collection) â†â†’ Cards (Tasks)
  \"Group related cards\"
  Manage related work together

Members (People) â†â†’ Cards (Tasks)
  \"Assign card to member\"
  Track individual workload
```

---

### 1.4 Consultant vs Client Roles

**Clear Separation of Responsibilities:**

The platform is designed with a clear division of labor between consultants (framework experts) and clients (implementation teams).

---

**Consultant Manages:**

**1. Dynamic Lists and Reference Structure:**

```
What Consultant Does:
âœ“ Creates compliance frameworks in workflows
âœ“ Exports frameworks to board references
âœ“ Updates reference structure when regulations change
âœ“ Maintains single source of truth
âœ“ Documents requirements and guidance

What Consultant Does NOT Do:
âœ— Create implementation tasks
âœ— Assign work to client team
âœ— Set project deadlines
âœ— Manage day-to-day execution

Example:
Consultant creates GDPR workflow with all articles
Exports to board â†’ Appears in References panel
Updates workflow when GDPR guidance changes
Client sees updated references automatically
```

**2. Reference Column Content:**

```
The References Column:
- First column on board (if enabled)
- Locked (cards cannot be moved)
- Contains compliance requirements
- Maintained by consultant
- Read-only for client

Consultant populates with:
- Regulatory requirements
- Control descriptions
- Evidence guidelines
- Policy templates
- Best practice documentation
```

**3. Compliance Requirement Trees:**

```
Consultant's Expertise:
â”œâ”€ Maps regulation structure
â”œâ”€ Breaks down requirements
â”œâ”€ Provides implementation guidance
â”œâ”€ Links related requirements
â””â”€ Updates when regulations change

Client's Benefit:
- Always have current requirements
- Understand what's needed
- Reference during implementation
- Confidence in compliance coverage
```

**Consultant Value Proposition:**

```
Consultant brings:
âœ“ Regulatory expertise
âœ“ Framework knowledge
âœ“ Best practices
âœ“ Consistency across clients
âœ“ Updates when regulations change

Consultant provides:
- The WHAT (requirements)
- The WHY (compliance rationale)
- The STRUCTURE (organization)
- The GUIDANCE (how-to recommendations)
```

---

**Client Manages:**

**1. Task Creation and Assignment:**

```
Client Responsibilities:
âœ“ Break requirements into specific tasks
âœ“ Assign tasks to team members
âœ“ Set task priorities
âœ“ Create task descriptions
âœ“ Add checklists and subtasks
âœ“ Update task status

Example:
Requirement (from reference): \"Implement MFA\"

Client creates tasks:
â”œâ”€ Task: Research MFA solutions (Assigned: IT Analyst)
â”œâ”€ Task: Get budget approval (Assigned: IT Manager)
â”œâ”€ Task: Purchase licenses (Assigned: Procurement)
â”œâ”€ Task: Deploy MFA (Assigned: System Admin)
â””â”€ Task: Train users (Assigned: Training Coordinator)
```

**2. Milestone Planning:**

```
Client Creates:
- Sprint schedules
- Phase timelines
- Release dates
- Audit deadlines

Client Tracks:
- Milestone progress
- On-time delivery
- Completion percentages
- Blocker identification

Example Milestones:
â”œâ”€ Phase 1: Assessment (Weeks 1-4)
â”œâ”€ Phase 2: Implementation (Weeks 5-12)
â”œâ”€ Phase 3: Testing (Weeks 13-16)
â””â”€ Phase 4: Audit (Week 17)
```

**3. Category Organization:**

```
Client Defines:
- How to classify tasks
- What categories to create
- Category colors and icons
- Category-based workflows

Example Categories:
â”œâ”€ ğŸ”´ Urgent
â”œâ”€ ğŸŸ¡ Important
â”œâ”€ ğŸŸ¢ Routine
â”œâ”€ ğŸ“„ Documentation
â”œâ”€ ğŸ’» Technical
â””â”€ ğŸ‘¥ Training
```

**4. Group Management:**

```
Client Creates Groups:
- Logically related task sets
- Project phases
- Work streams
- Vendor engagements

Example:
Group: \"MFA Implementation\"
â”œâ”€ Contains 8 related tasks
â”œâ”€ Shows 62% complete
â”œâ”€ All tasks in this group visible together
â””â”€ Move group through board stages together
```

**5. Progress Tracking:**

```
Client Monitors:
âœ“ Task completion rates
âœ“ Team velocity
âœ“ Milestone progress
âœ“ Blocker identification
âœ“ Resource allocation
âœ“ Timeline adherence

Client Reports:
- Weekly progress updates
- Sprint retrospectives
- Risk identification
- Resource needs
- Completion forecasts
```

**Client Value Proposition:**

```
Client controls:
âœ“ Execution plan
âœ“ Resource allocation
âœ“ Timeline and priorities
âœ“ Internal processes
âœ“ Team structure

Client autonomy:
- The WHO (assignments)
- The WHEN (deadlines)
- The HOW (implementation approach)
- The ORGANIZATION (task structure)
```

---

**Collaborative Model:**

```
Consultant + Client = Successful Compliance

Consultant:                    Client:
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”          â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”

â”‚ Requirements     â”‚          â”‚ Tasks            â”‚
â”‚ Structure        â”‚          â”‚ Assignments      â”‚
â”‚ Guidance         â”‚          â”‚ Timelines        â”‚
â”‚ Updates          â”‚          â”‚ Progress         â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜          â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

         â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
                    â”‚
                    â–¼
           â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
           â”‚  Board Platform  â”‚
           â”‚  â”œâ”€ References   â”‚ (Consultant)
           â”‚  â””â”€ Workspace    â”‚ (Client)
           â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

References: Consultant's domain (compliance framework)
Workspace: Client's domain (implementation execution)

Both visible to both parties
Clear boundaries
Mutual visibility
Collaborative success
```

**Real-World Example:**

```
Scenario: ISO 27001 Implementation

Consultant:
1. Creates ISO 27001 workflow (93 controls)
2. Exports to board
3. Controls appear in References panel
4. Adds implementation guidance notes
5. Updates when ISO updates

Client:
1. Reviews controls in References
2. Creates tasks for each control:
   - \"Draft access control policy\"
   - \"Configure MFA for admins\"
   - \"Implement encryption at rest\"
3. Assigns tasks to IT, HR, Legal teams
4. Sets up Sprint 1-6 milestones
5. Creates categories: Critical, High, Medium, Low
6. Groups tasks by domain
7. Tracks progress weekly
8. Moves tasks through columns as work completes

Result:
- Consultant ensures all 93 controls covered
- Client implements at their own pace
- Mutual visibility into progress
- Audit-ready documentation
- Successful certification
```

## CHAPTER 2: ACCESSING BOARDS

Navigate to boards and understand the board library.

### 2.1 Boards Navigation

**From the Platform:**

**Primary Entry Point:**

```
Main Navigation Bar:
[Templates] [Workflows] [Boards] [Documentation]
                          â†‘
                    Click here
```

**From Any Page:**

```
Top Navigation:
- Always accessible
- "Boards" link visible globally
- Click to go to Board Library
- Current location highlights in nav bar
```

**From Workflow (After Export):**

```
Workflow â†’ Export to Board â†’ Board Created
                                    â†“
                        "Open Board" button appears
                                    â†“
                            Takes you directly to board
```

**Direct URL:**

```
https://yourplatform.com/boards.html
(Bookmark this for quick access)
```

**Board Library View:**

```
When you click "Boards," you arrive at the Board Library:
```

### 2.2 Board Library

**Board Card Display:**

Each board displays as a card in a grid layout with key information at a glance.

**Board Card Structure:**

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  ISO 27001 Implementation               â”‚ â† Board Name
â”‚  Acme Corp certification project        â”‚ â† Description
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚  Progress: â–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–‘â–‘ 75%               â”‚ â† Progress Bar
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  ğŸ“ 45 tasks  â”‚  ğŸ‘¥ 8 members           â”‚ â† Stats
â”‚  âœ“ 34 done   â”‚  ğŸ¯ 3 milestones        â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  Last updated: 2 hours ago              â”‚ â† Timestamp
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

**Board Name and Description:**

```
Board Name:
- Large, bold text
- Clearly identifies project
- Clickable (opens board)

Description:
- 1-2 line summary
- Project context
- Helps distinguish between boards
- Optional but recommended

Example:
Name: "Q1 2024 Security Initiatives"
Description: "Quarterly security projects and compliance updates"
```

**Progress Bars:**

```
Visual Progress Indicator:

â–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–‘â–‘ 75%

Calculation:
Progress = (Done tasks / Total tasks) Ã— 100%

Example:
34 tasks done / 45 total tasks = 75.6% â†’ displayed as 76%

Color Coding:
0-33%:  ğŸ”´ Red (not much progress)
34-66%: ğŸŸ¡ Yellow (making progress)
67-99%: ğŸŸ¢ Green (almost done)
100%:   ğŸ”µ Blue (complete)
```

**Task Count:**

```
ğŸ“ 45 tasks

Shows total number of cards on board
Includes tasks in all columns
Updated in real-time
Quick gauge of board size
```

**Member Count:**

```
ğŸ‘¥ 8 members

Shows number of people with board access
Includes all roles (admin, member, viewer)
Click to see member list
Useful for team coordination
```

**Percentage Complete:**

```
âœ“ 34 done (75%)

Combines:
- Number of completed tasks
- Percentage calculation
- Visual progress bar

Quick status check without opening board
```

**Click to Open:**

```
Interaction:
- Click anywhere on card â†’ Opens board
- Hover: Slight elevation/shadow effect
- Cursor changes to pointer
- Smooth transition to board view

Opens board in same tab
(Use Ctrl+Click to open in new tab)
```


**Sorting and Filtering (if available):**

```
Sort By:
- Last Updated (default)
- Name (A-Z)
- Progress (high to low)
- Created Date

Filter By:
- My Boards
- Shared with Me
- Archived
- By Member
```

### 2.3 Creating Boards

**Two Creation Methods:**

1. **From Scratch** - Empty board, build your own structure
2. **From Workflow Export** - Pre-populated with compliance framework

---

**Method 1: From Scratch (Manual Creation)**

**Step-by-Step:**

1. **Click "Create Board" Button**

```
Location: Top-right of Board Library
Button: [+ Create Board]
Action: Opens creation modal
```

2. **Fill in Board Details**

```
Create Board Modal:
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  Create New Board                    [Ã—]â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  Board Name: (required)                 â”‚
â”‚  [_________________________________]    â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  Description: (optional)                â”‚
â”‚  [_________________________________]    â”‚
â”‚  [_________________________________]    â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  â˜‘ Include References Column           â”‚
â”‚     (For compliance frameworks)         â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚            [Cancel]  [Create Board]     â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

3. **Board Name (Required)**

```
Best Practices:
âœ“ Clear and descriptive
âœ“ Include project/client name
âœ“ Include timeframe if relevant

Examples:
âœ“ "Acme Corp - ISO 27001 Implementation"
âœ“ "Q1 2024 Security Projects"
âœ“ "Website Redesign - Sprint 1"

Avoid:
âœ— "Board 1" (too vague)
âœ— "ISO" (incomplete context)
âœ— "New Board" (default, not descriptive)
```

4. **Description (Optional but Recommended)**

```
What to Include:
- Project purpose
- Timeline
- Key stakeholders
- Scope

Example:
"12-month ISO 27001 certification project for Acme Corp's 
EU operations. Includes 93 controls across 4 domains. 
Target completion: Q4 2024."

Benefits:
- Helps team understand context
- Useful when managing many boards
- Good for reporting
```

5. **Include References Column (Checkbox)**

```
â˜‘ Include References Column

What This Does:
- Adds a locked "References" column (first column)
- Column cannot be deleted
- Cards in this column cannot be moved
- Ideal for compliance frameworks

When to Enable:
âœ“ Compliance projects (ISO, GDPR, SOC 2, etc.)
âœ“ Need to maintain reference materials
âœ“ Want locked documentation column

When to Skip:
âœ— General project management
âœ— Agile software development
âœ— Simple task tracking
```

6. **Create Board**

```
Click [Create Board] button:
- Board is created immediately
- Redirects to new board
- Board appears with default columns:
  - References (if enabled)
  - To Do
  - In Progress
  - Review
  - Done
- Empty (no cards yet)
- Ready for task creation
```

**After Creation:**

```
New Empty Board:

â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  Acme Corp - ISO 27001 Implementation               â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚ Ref    â”‚ To Do  â”‚ In Progâ”‚ Review â”‚ Done            â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤

Start adding tasks with [+ Add Task] button
```

---

**Method 2: From Workflow Export (Automated)**

**The Power of Workflow Integration:**

This is the recommended method for compliance projects as it auto-populates your board with the entire compliance framework.

**Step-by-Step:**

1. **Start from Workflow**

```
Open a workflow:
- Navigate to Workflows
- Select workflow (e.g., "ISO 27001:2022 Framework")
- Ensure workflow is complete and saved
```

2. **Click Export Button**

```
Location: Top navigation in workflow
Button: [Export to Board]

Export Modal Opens:
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  Export Workflow to Board            [Ã—]â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  Export Method:                         â”‚
â”‚  â— Full Workflow                        â”‚
â”‚  â—‹ Selected Unit                        â”‚
â”‚  â—‹ By Tag                               â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  Destination:                           â”‚
â”‚  â— Create New Board                     â”‚
â”‚  â—‹ Add to Existing Board                â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  Board Name:                            â”‚
â”‚  [Acme Corp - ISO 27001 Implementation] â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  Export Options:                        â”‚
â”‚  â˜‘ Include Descriptions                 â”‚
â”‚  â˜‘ Include Links                        â”‚
â”‚  â˜‘ Include Images                       â”‚
â”‚  â˜‘ Include Notes                        â”‚
â”‚  â˜‘ Sync future workflow updates         â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚         [Cancel]  [Export to Board]     â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

3. **Configure Export**

```
Choose Export Method:
- Full Workflow: All 93 controls (most common)
- Selected Unit: Just one section (e.g., "Access Controls")
- By Tag: Filtered subset (e.g., [Critical] tagged items)

Choose Destination:
- Create New Board: Fresh board (recommended)
- Add to Existing: Append to existing board

Name Your Board:
- Auto-suggests: "[Workflow Name]"
- Edit as needed
- Example: "Acme Corp - ISO 27001 Implementation"

Export Options:
- Include all content (recommended)
- Enable sync (updates when workflow changes)
```

4. **Execute Export**

```
Click [Export to Board]:
- Progress indicator appears
- Exports all units from workflow
- Creates board structure
- Populates references column

Progress:
â–“â–“â–“â–“â–“â–“â–“â–“â–‘â–‘ 80% (75/93 units exported)

Takes 5-30 seconds depending on workflow size
```

5. **Board Created Automatically**

```
Success Message:
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  âœ“ Board Created Successfully           â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚  93 units exported to:                  â”‚
â”‚  "Acme Corp - ISO 27001 Implementation" â”‚
â”‚                                         â”‚
â”‚     [Open Board]  [Stay in Workflow]    â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

Click [Open Board] to go to new board
```

6. **Board Opens with Content**

```
Exported Board Structure:

â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  Acme Corp - ISO 27001 Implementation               â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚ References  â”‚ To Do  â”‚ In Progâ”‚ Review â”‚ Done      â”‚
â”‚ (Read-Only) â”‚        â”‚        â”‚        â”‚           â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤

â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”´â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”´â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”´â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”´â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

References column: Full ISO 27001 structure
Other columns: Empty, ready for tasks
```

**What Gets Exported:**

```
From Workflow â†’ To Board References:

âœ“ All unit names
âœ“ Full hierarchy structure
âœ“ Descriptions
âœ“ Display IDs (A.5.1, A.5.2, etc.)
âœ“ Icons
âœ“ Tags (become board labels)
âœ“ Links (policy references)
âœ“ Images (diagrams, screenshots)
âœ“ Notes (implementation guidance)

References Column = Complete compliance framework
Ready to reference while creating implementation tasks
```

---

**Comparison: From Scratch vs From Export**

```
From Scratch:
âœ“ Full control over structure
âœ“ Simple setup
âœ“ Good for general projects
âœ— No pre-populated content
âœ— Manual entry required
Use Case: General project management

From Export:
âœ“ Auto-populated references
âœ“ Complete framework included
âœ“ Linked to source workflow
âœ“ Syncs with workflow updates
âœ— Requires existing workflow
Use Case: Compliance projects
```

**Best Practice:**

```
Compliance Projects:
1. Create template (one-time)
2. Create workflow from template
3. Populate workflow with requirements
4. Export workflow to board
5. Client creates tasks on board

General Projects:
1. Create board from scratch
2. Add columns for your workflow
3. Create tasks directly
4. Manage with milestones and categories
```

**Board Name (Display):**

```

- Large, prominent text
- Top-left of header
- Shows board title

Example: "ISO 27001 Implementation"
Subtitle: "Acme Corp certification" (if provided)

- Click to edit board name
- Modal opens for editing
- Update name and description
```

**Adding Members:**

```
Click [+ Add Member]:

1. Enter email address
2. Select role (Admin/Member/Viewer)
3. Click [Invite]
4. Member receives invitation
5. Joins board after accepting

Or:

Select from existing users:
- List of platform users
- Check to add
- Immediate access
```

**Theme Toggle (ğŸŒ“):**

```
Purpose: Switch between light and dark themes

Click to toggle:
Light Mode â‡„ Dark Mode

Light Mode:
- White background
- Dark text
- High contrast
- Good for bright environments

Dark Mode:
- Dark background
- Light text
- Reduces eye strain
- Good for low-light environments

Preference saved:
- Per-user setting
- Persists across sessions
- Works on all boards
- Platform-wide setting
```

**Progress Indicators:**

```
Progress Calculation:
Progress = (Linked tasks marked done / Total linked tasks) Ã— 100%

Example:
Milestone "Sprint 1":
- 20 tasks linked to milestone
- 12 tasks marked done
- Progress: 12/20 = 60%

Display: â–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–‘â–‘â–‘â–‘ 60%

Real-time Update:
- Mark task done â†’ Progress increases
- Uncheck done â†’ Progress decreases
```

**Filtering by Milestone:**

```
Click on milestone card:
- Board filters to show only tasks in that milestone
- Other tasks hidden
- Filter banner appears at top
- Click [X] to clear filter

Example:
Filter: Sprint 1 [Ã—]
Showing 20 of 45 tasks
```

**Group-Level Progress:**

```
Progress Calculation:
Progress = (Done tasks in group / Total tasks in group) Ã— 100%

Example:

- 5 tasks in group
- 2 tasks done
- Progress: 2/5 = 40%

Display: â–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–‘â–‘â–‘â–‘â–‘â–‘ 40%

Visual Grouping:
- Tasks in same group can be visually connected
- Helps see related work
- Track sub-project progress
```

**Horizontal Scrolling:**

```
If many columns:
- Scroll horizontally to see all
- Mouse wheel scroll
- Drag scrollbar
- Touch swipe on mobile

No limit to number of columns
Create as many as needed for your workflow
```

**Default Columns:**

```
New boards start with 4 columns:

1. To Do
   - Backlog
   - Not started
   - Planning

2. In Progress
   - Active work
   - Current focus
   - WIP limit useful here

3. Review
   - Needs checking
   - Awaiting approval
   - Quality control

4. Done
   - Completed work
   - Achieved
   - Success

Fully customizable - rename, reorder, add, delete
```

**Column Structure:**

```
Column Header:
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ In Progress    â”‚ â† Column Name
â”‚ (8 tasks)      â”‚ â† Task Count
â”‚ WIP: 8/10 âš ï¸   â”‚ â† WIP Limit (if set)
â”‚      â‹®         â”‚ â† Column Menu
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

â”‚ â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â” â”‚
```

**Column Menus:**

```
Click â‹® (three dots) â†’ Column Menu:

â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ Rename Column       â”‚
â”‚ Set WIP Limit       â”‚
â”‚ Change Color        â”‚
â”‚ Move Left           â”‚
â”‚ Move Right          â”‚
â”‚ â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€      â”‚
â”‚ Delete Column       â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

Actions:
- Rename: Change column name
- WIP Limit: Set max tasks allowed
- Color: Visual distinction
- Move: Reorder columns
- Delete: Remove column (moves tasks to first column)
```

**Card Counts:**

```
Display: (8 tasks)

Shows number of cards in column
Updates in real-time:
- Add task â†’ Count increases
- Move task out â†’ Count decreases
- Delete task â†’ Count decreases

Helpful for:
- Visualizing workload
- Balancing work across columns
- Identifying bottlenecks
```

**WIP Limits (Work In Progress):**

```
Purpose: Prevent overload, maintain flow

Set WIP Limit:
Column Menu â†’ Set WIP Limit â†’ Enter number

Example:
In Progress: WIP Limit = 10

Display:
In Progress
(12 tasks)
WIP: 12/10 âš ï¸

Warning (âš ï¸) when exceeded:
- Orange/red badge
- Visual indicator
- Soft limit (not enforced)
- Encourages moving tasks forward

Benefits:
- Prevents too much parallel work
- Encourages finishing before starting
- Improves flow and focus
- Identifies bottlenecks
```

**Drag and Drop:**

```
Move cards between columns:

1. Click and hold card
2. Drag to target column
3. Drop in column
4. Card moves

Visual Feedback:
- Card lifts (shadow effect)
- Target column highlights
- Drop zones show
- Smooth animation

Keyboard Alternative:
- Select card
- Press Ctrl+â†’ (move right)
- Press Ctrl+â† (move left)
```

**Slide-Out Panel (Toggle):**

```
Toggle Button: [â—€] or [â–¶]

Click to toggle:
[â—€] Close panel (more space for columns)
[â–¶] Open panel (see references)

Panel States:
- Open: Takes ~25% of screen width
- Closed: Hidden, full width for columns

Preference saved per user
```

**Tree Structure Display:**

```
Hierarchy Display:

â–¼ ISO 27001:2022
  â”œâ”€ â–¼ Organizational Controls
  â”‚  â”œâ”€ A.5.1 Information Security Policy
  â”‚  â”œâ”€ A.5.2 Information Security Roles
  â”‚  â””â”€ A.5.3 Separation of Duties
  â”‚
  â”œâ”€ â–¶ People Controls (collapsed)
  â”‚
  â”œâ”€ â–¶ Physical Controls (collapsed)

  â””â”€ â–¶ Technological Controls (collapsed)

â–¶ = Collapsed

```

**Mode Toggle (Creation/Reference):**

```
Two Modes:

[Creation Mode] [Reference Mode]
      â†‘              â†‘
  (Selected)    (Not selected)

Creation Mode:
- Can add connections to tasks
- Link tasks to reference items
- Show which tasks address which requirements

Reference Mode:
- View-only
- Browse compliance framework
- Read descriptions and guidance

Most users stay in Reference Mode
```

**Search Bar:**

```
Search within dynamic list:

â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ ğŸ” Search references... [Ã—]     â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

Type to search:
- Unit names
- Display IDs
- Descriptions

Results highlight:
- Matching items expand automatically
- Search term highlighted in yellow
- Clear search with [Ã—]

Example:
Search: "MFA"
Results: Highlights "Multi-Factor Authentication" items
```

**Collapse/Expand Controls:**

```
Control Buttons:

[â–¼ Expand All] [â–² Collapse All]

Expand All:
- Opens all tree nodes
- See full structure
- Useful for overview

Collapse All:
- Closes all tree nodes
- Clean view
- See only top-level items

Keyboard:
- Space: Expand/collapse selected item
- â†’ : Expand
- â† : Collapse
```

**Task/Connection Nodes:**

```
Show Task Connections:

â–¼ A.5.1 Information Security Policy
  â”‚
  â”œâ”€ ğŸ“‹ Draft InfoSec Policy (To Do)
  â”œâ”€ ğŸ“‹ Get legal review (In Progress)
  â””â”€ ğŸ“‹ Publish to intranet (Done)
     â†‘
  Tasks linked to this requirement

Benefits:
- See which tasks address which requirements
- Ensure requirement coverage
- Track requirement completion
- Audit trail
```

**Dynamic List Features:**

```
Features:
âœ“ Full workflow structure (read-only)
âœ“ Expand/collapse navigation
âœ“ Search functionality
âœ“ Link tasks to reference items
âœ“ See task connections
âœ“ Compliance coverage tracking
âœ“ Syncs with source workflow
âœ“ Always current

Use Cases:
- Reference compliance requirements
- Ensure coverage
- Link tasks to requirements
- Audit preparation
- Team guidance
```

```
- Rapid brainstorming
- Sprint planning
- Quick capture
```

---

## CHAPTER 4: WORKING WITH COLUMNS

Customize your workflow states with flexible column management.

### 4.1 Understanding Columns

**What are Columns:**

Columns represent the stages or states that tasks move through during their lifecycle.

**Kanban Column Concept:**

```
Traditional Workflow:
Task created â†’ Task in progress â†’ Task reviewed â†’ Task completed

Kanban Board Columns:
[To Do] â†’ [In Progress] â†’ [Review] â†’ [Done]

Each column = One state
Cards (tasks) move left to right as they progress
```

**Workflow States:**

```
Column = State of Work

Examples by Project Type:

Software Development:
Backlog â†’ To Do â†’ Development â†’ Code Review â†’ QA â†’ Staging â†’ Production

Compliance Implementation:
Not Started â†’ Planning â†’ Implementation â†’ Documentation â†’ Review â†’ Complete

Manufacturing:
Design â†’ Prototype â†’ Testing â†’ Quality Check â†’ Production â†’ Shipped

Content Creation:
Ideas â†’ Outline â†’ Draft â†’ Editing â†’ Review â†’ Published
```

**Left to Right Progression:**

```
Standard Flow:

â†â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â†’
Start                                       End

[Backlog] â†’ [To Do] â†’ [Doing] â†’ [Done]

Conventions:
- Left: Early stages
- Middle: Active work
- Right: Completion

Visual Flow:
- Cards enter from left
- Move rightward as progress
- End at rightmost column (typically "Done")
```

**Unlimited Columns:**

```
Create as many as needed:

Simple: 3 columns
[To Do] [Doing] [Done]

Standard: 4 columns
[To Do] [In Progress] [Review] [Done]

Complex: 8+ columns
[Backlog] [To Do] [In Progress] [Code Review] [QA Testing] [UAT] [Staging] [Done]

No artificial limits
Adapt to your process
```

**Customizable Names:**

```
Not limited to default names
Rename to match your terminology:

âœ“ "Backlog" or "Ideas" or "Queue"
âœ“ "In Progress" or "Doing" or "Active Work"
âœ“ "Review" or "QA" or "Approval"
âœ“ "Done" or "Complete" or "Deployed"

Use terms your team understands
```

**Reorderable:**

```
Change column sequence:
- Drag column headers to reorder
- Or use column menu (Move Left/Right)

Example:
Before: [To Do] [Done] [In Progress]
(Wrong order!)

After: [To Do] [In Progress] [Done]
(Correct flow!)

Order matters for intuitive workflow
```

---

### 4.2 Default Columns

New boards start with 4 standard columns optimized for most projects.

**To Do:**

**Purpose:** Task backlog and entry point

```
Characteristics:
- Leftmost column (after References if present)
- Where new tasks start
- Not yet assigned or scheduled
- Planning stage

Typical Contents:
- Newly created tasks
- Unassigned work
- Future tasks
- Ideas and possibilities

Example Tasks:
â”œâ”€ "Draft MFA policy"
â”œâ”€ "Research encryption solutions"
â”œâ”€ "Schedule security training"
â””â”€ "Review firewall rules"

State: Not started, planning phase
```

**When to Move FROM To Do:**

```
Move to next column when:
âœ“ Task is assigned to someone
âœ“ Work is about to begin
âœ“ Resources are available
âœ“ Dependencies are resolved

Keep IN To Do when:
- Not ready to start
- Waiting for something
- Lower priority
- Still planning
```

---

**In Progress:**

**Purpose:** Active work happening now

```
Characteristics:
- Middle column (active work zone)
- WIP limits most useful here
- Indicates current team focus
- High-attention area

Typical Contents:
- Tasks being worked on right now
- Assigned and active
- Team's current focus
- Today's work

Example Tasks:
â”œâ”€ "Writing access control policy" (Sarah, 60% done)
â”œâ”€ "Configuring MFA in Azure AD" (John, in progress)
â””â”€ "Installing encryption software" (Mike, started today)

State: Active, in progress, being worked on
```

**WIP Limit Recommendation:**

```
Set WIP limit = Number of team members Ã— 1.5

Examples:
- 4 team members â†’ WIP limit: 6 tasks
- 8 team members â†’ WIP limit: 12 tasks

Prevents:
- Too many concurrent tasks
- Context switching
- Unfinished work piling up

Encourages:
- Finishing before starting
- Focus on completion
- Better flow
```

---

**Review:**

**Purpose:** Quality check and approval

```
Characteristics:
- Pre-completion stage
- Awaiting verification
- Quality gate
- Approval checkpoint

Typical Contents:
- Completed work awaiting review
- Documents pending approval
- Code in code review
- Deliverables before acceptance

Example Tasks:
â”œâ”€ "InfoSec Policy v1.0" (Awaiting legal review)
â”œâ”€ "MFA Configuration" (Awaiting security approval)
â””â”€ "Training Materials" (Awaiting manager approval)

State: Done with work, pending verification
```

**Who Reviews:**

```
Reviewers depend on task type:

Technical Tasks â†’ Technical Lead
Documentation â†’ Legal/Compliance
Policies â†’ Management
Code â†’ Senior Developer
Designs â†’ Design Lead

Assign reviewers:
- In task assignments
- In task comments
- Via @ mentions
```

**Review Process:**

```
1. Worker moves task to Review column
2. Reviewer notified (if notifications enabled)
3. Reviewer checks task
4. Options:
   âœ“ Approve â†’ Move to Done
   âœ— Request changes â†’ Move back to In Progress
   ? Need info â†’ Add comment, keep in Review

Fast track compliance:
Ensures quality before marking complete
```

---

**Done:**

**Purpose:** Completed and approved work

```
Characteristics:
- Rightmost column
- Finished tasks
- Approved and accepted
- Achievement tracking

Typical Contents:
- Completed and approved tasks
- Delivered work
- Achieved milestones
- Success stories

Example Tasks:
â”œâ”€ "âœ“ InfoSec Policy Published" (Completed Jan 15)
â”œâ”€ "âœ“ MFA Deployed Company-Wide" (Completed Jan 20)
â””â”€ "âœ“ Security Training Complete" (Completed Jan 25)

State: Finished, approved, delivered
```

**Done Means Done:**

```
Tasks in Done column should be:
âœ“ Work completed
âœ“ Quality verified
âœ“ Approved by reviewer
âœ“ Delivered to stakeholder
âœ“ No further action needed

Not Done:
âœ— "90% complete" â†’ Keep in In Progress or Review
âœ— "Waiting for approval" â†’ Keep in Review
âœ— "Almost done" â†’ Not done yet
```

**Progress Calculation:**

```
Board Progress = Tasks in Done / Total Tasks

Example:
- To Do: 10 tasks
- In Progress: 5 tasks
- Review: 3 tasks
- Done: 27 tasks

Total: 45 tasks
Done: 27 tasks
Progress: 27/45 = 60%

Done column drives board completion percentage
```

---

### 4.3 Adding Custom Columns

**When to Add Columns:**

```
Add columns when:
âœ“ Need more granular workflow states
âœ“ Have specific approval stages
âœ“ Separate different types of work
âœ“ Compliance requires specific stages
âœ“ Team needs more clarity

Examples:
- Add "QA Testing" between Review and Done
- Add "Backlog" before To Do
- Add "Deployed" after Done
- Add "Blocked" for stuck tasks
```

**How to Add:**

**Method 1: Plus Button**

```
1. Scroll to far right of columns
2. Click [+] button
3. Add Column modal opens
4. Enter column name
5. Choose position
6. Click [Add Column]

Column appears immediately
```

**Method 2: Column Menu**

```
Some implementations:
- Any column menu â†’ Add Column After
- Creates column immediately after current
- Skip position selection
```

**Add Column Modal:**

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  Add Column                      [Ã—]â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚  Column Name: (required)            â”‚
â”‚  [QA Testing___________________]    â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚  Position:                          â”‚
â”‚  â— At end (default)                 â”‚
â”‚  â—‹ After "In Progress"              â”‚
â”‚  â—‹ Before "Done"                    â”‚
â”‚  â—‹ At beginning                     â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚  Color: (optional)                  â”‚
â”‚  ğŸ”µ ğŸŸ¢ ğŸŸ¡ ğŸ”´ ğŸŸ£ ğŸŸ¤ âš«              â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚  WIP Limit: (optional)              â”‚
â”‚  [____] tasks (blank = no limit)    â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚       [Cancel]  [Add Column]        â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

**Positioning Options:**

```
At End (Default):
Before: [To Do] [In Progress] [Review] [Done]
After:  [To Do] [In Progress] [Review] [Done] [QA Testing]

After "In Progress":
Before: [To Do] [In Progress] [Review] [Done]
After:  [To Do] [In Progress] [QA Testing] [Review] [Done]

Before "Done":
Same as "After Review" in most cases

At Beginning:
Before: [To Do] [In Progress] [Review] [Done]
After:  [Backlog] [To Do] [In Progress] [Review] [Done]
```

**Immediate Availability:**

```
After creation:
âœ“ Column appears on board
âœ“ Can add tasks immediately
âœ“ Can drag tasks to it
âœ“ Included in column count
âœ“ Appears in column selection dropdowns

Auto-saves:
- No manual save needed
- Column persists immediately
- Visible to all board members
```

### 4.4 Renaming Columns

**When to Rename:**

```
Reasons to rename:
- Initial name unclear
- Team prefers different terminology
- Process changes
- Better clarity needed

Example:
"In Progress" â†’ "Active Development" (more specific)
"Review" â†’ "Code Review" (clarifies type of review)
"Done" â†’ "Deployed to Production" (explicit outcome)
```

**How to Rename:**

```
1. Click column menu (â‹®)
2. Select "Rename Column"
3. Enter new name
4. Press Enter or click Save
5. Column renames immediately

Or:

Double-click column name (if enabled)
- Inline editing
- Type new name
- Press Enter
- Updates immediately
```

**Rename Column Dialog:**

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”

```

**Updates Immediately:**

```
Before:
[To Do] [In Progress] [Done]
         â†‘
    Rename this

After:
[To Do] [Active Development] [Done]
         â†‘
    New name shows immediately
```

**Historical Data Preserved:**

```
Activity Log Maintains Context:

Before Rename:
"John moved task to In Progress" (Jan 10, 10:00 AM)

After Rename to "Active Development":
"John moved task to Active Development" (Jan 10, 10:00 AM)
(Some implementations update retroactively)

Or:
"John moved task to In Progress (now 'Active Development')"
(Shows both names for clarity)

Cards in column:
- Remain in column
- Not affected by rename
- Continue working normally
```

### 4.5 Setting WIP Limits

**What are WIP Limits:**

```
WIP = Work In Progress

WIP Limit = Maximum number of tasks allowed in a column

Purpose:
- Prevent overload
- Maintain focus
- Encourage completion before starting new work
- Identify bottlenecks
```

**How to Set:**

```
1. Click column menu (â‹®)
2. Select "Set WIP Limit"
3. Enter numeric limit
4. Click [Save]
5. Limit applies immediately

Dialog:
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  Set WIP Limit                   [Ã—]â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚  Column: "In Progress"              â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚  Maximum tasks allowed:             â”‚
â”‚  [10____]                           â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚  Current tasks in column: 8         â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚  â˜ Block new tasks when limit hit  â”‚
â”‚     (Soft limit - warning only)     â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚       [Cancel]  [Set Limit]         â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

**Visual Warning When Exceeded:**

```
Column with WIP Limit:

Normal (Under Limit):
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ In Progress    â”‚
â”‚ (8 tasks)      â”‚
â”‚ WIP: 8/10 âœ“    â”‚ â† Green indicator
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

Exceeded (Over Limit):
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ In Progress    â”‚
â”‚ (12 tasks)     â”‚
â”‚ WIP: 12/10 âš ï¸  â”‚ â† Orange/red warning
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

**Orange Badge on Column Header:**

```
Visual Indicators:

[In Progress (12) âš ï¸]
                   â†‘
            Warning badge

Color changes:
- Green: Under limit
- Orange: At limit
- Red: Significantly over limit

Purpose: Visual reminder to finish work before starting more
```

**Soft Limit (Not Enforced):**

```
Soft Limit = Warning, not blocking

You CAN still:
âœ“ Add more tasks to column
âœ“ Drag tasks to column
âœ“ Move tasks beyond limit

System just warns you:
"WIP limit exceeded. Consider finishing existing tasks first."

Hard Limit (if enabled):
âœ— Blocks new tasks when limit reached
âœ— Cannot drag tasks to full column
(Rarely used - too restrictive)
```

**Recommended WIP Limits:**

```
Formula:
WIP Limit = Team Size Ã— 1.5 to 2

Examples:
- 4 developers â†’ WIP: 6-8 tasks
- 2 developers â†’ WIP: 3-4 tasks
- 10 team members â†’ WIP: 15-20 tasks

Adjust based on:
- Task complexity (complex tasks â†’ lower WIP)
- Task duration (short tasks â†’ higher WIP)
- Team experience (new teams â†’ lower WIP)
```

**Benefits:**

```
Prevents:
âœ— Context switching
âœ— Unfinished work accumulation
âœ— Bottlenecks going unnoticed
âœ— Team overload

Encourages:
âœ“ Finishing before starting
âœ“ Focus and completion
âœ“ Identifying blockers
âœ“ Better flow

Result:
- More tasks actually completed
- Less stress
- Better quality
```

---

### 4.6 Deleting Columns

**When to Delete:**

```
Reasons to delete:
- Column no longer needed
- Process simplified
- Wrong column created
- Workflow changed

Example:
Had "Staging" column for testing
Moved to continuous deployment
"Staging" column obsolete â†’ Delete
```

**How to Delete:**

```
1. Click column menu (â‹®)
2. Select "Delete Column"
3. Confirmation dialog appears
4. Confirm deletion
5. Column removed immediately

Cannot Delete If:
- Only 1 column remains (board must have at least one)
- Column is "References" (locked column)
```

**Delete Column Dialog:**

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  Delete Column?                  [Ã—]â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚  Delete column "QA Testing"?        â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚  âš ï¸ This column has 5 tasks         â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚  Tasks will be moved to:            â”‚
â”‚  [To Do â–¼] (select destination)     â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚  This action cannot be undone.      â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚       [Cancel]  [Delete Column]     â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

**Cards Move to First Column:**

```
Before Delete:
[To Do] [In Progress] [QA Testing] [Done]
                       â†‘
                   5 tasks here

Delete "QA Testing" â†’

After Delete:
[To Do] [In Progress] [Done]
   â†‘
5 tasks moved here (default)

Or:
Choose destination column in delete dialog
Tasks move there instead
```

**Confirmation Required:**

```
Safety measures:
- Must click through confirmation
- Shows task count in column
- Option to choose task destination
- Admin permission may be required

Prevents accidental deletion
```

**Permanent Action:**

```
Cannot undo column deletion

After deletion:
âœ— Column structure removed
âœ— Column configuration lost
âœ— Historical activity logs keep old column name references

âœ“ Tasks preserved (moved to another column)
âœ“ Task data intact
âœ“ Can recreate column if needed (but configuration is lost)

Think carefully before deleting
```

---

### 4.7 The References Column

**Special Column for Compliance Frameworks:**

The References column is a unique, locked column designed specifically for compliance and regulatory frameworks.

**Special Properties:**

**1. First Column (If Enabled):**

```
Board Layout with References:

[References] [To Do] [In Progress] [Review] [Done]
     â†‘
 Always first
```

**2. Locked (Cards Cannot Leave):**

```
References Column Behavior:

âœ“ Can add cards to References
âœ“ Can view cards in References
âœ— CANNOT drag cards out of References
âœ— CANNOT move References cards to other columns

Purpose:
- Keep reference materials separate
- Prevent accidental mixing with execution tasks
- Maintain clean reference library
```

**3. Reference Materials Only:**

```
Typical Reference Column Contents:

Compliance Requirements:
â”œâ”€ "GDPR Article 32: Security of Processing"
â”œâ”€ "ISO 27001 A.9.4.3: MFA Requirement"
â”œâ”€ "NIST CSF PR.AC-7: Access Control"
â””â”€ ... (more requirements)

NOT for execution tasks:
âœ— "Draft MFA policy" (this goes in To Do)
âœ— "Configure encryption" (this goes in To Do/In Progress)

References = WHAT to do
Other columns = WHO, WHEN, HOW
```

**4. Filter Activation Point:**

```
Click reference item:
- Filters board to show only linked tasks
- See which tasks address this requirement
- Track requirement coverage

Example:
Click "A.9.4.3: MFA Requirement" in References
â†“
Board filters to show:
- "Research MFA solutions" (To Do)
- "Purchase MFA licenses" (In Progress)
- "Deploy MFA" (Done)

All tasks linked to this requirement visible
Others hidden
```

**5. Cannot Be Deleted:**

```
References column is permanent (if enabled at board creation)

Attempting to delete:
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  Cannot Delete References Column    â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚  The References column is locked    â”‚
â”‚  and cannot be deleted.             â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚  It maintains compliance framework  â”‚
â”‚  structure and requirement links.   â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚            [OK]                      â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

Protection for compliance integrity
```

**6. Consultant Controlled:**

```
Typical Access:
- Consultant: Can add/edit References
- Client: Read-only access to References
- Client: Full control of other columns

Permission Model:
References Column: Consultant domain
Other Columns: Client domain

Prevents:
- Client accidentally deleting requirements
- Framework structure corruption
- Compliance gaps
```

---

**Purpose of References Column:**

**Store Compliance Requirements:**

```
Populate with:
- Regulatory requirements (GDPR articles, ISO controls)
- Compliance obligations
- Legal requirements
- Standards and frameworks
- Policy requirements

Example:
â”œâ”€ "GDPR Art. 5(1)(a): Lawfulness"
â”œâ”€ "GDPR Art. 5(1)(b): Purpose Limitation"
â”œâ”€ "GDPR Art. 5(1)(c): Data Minimization"
â””â”€ ... (all GDPR principles)

Complete compliance reference library
```

**Hold Regulation References:**

```
Reference card contains:
- Requirement title
- Regulatory source (article, clause)
- Description (what is required)
- Implementation guidance
- Links to official regulation text
- Evidence requirements

Team references while creating implementation tasks
```

**Maintain Source Documentation:**

```
References = Single Source of Truth

Workflow (Source):
- Consultant updates when regulations change
- Syncs to board references
- Always current

Board References:
- Reflects current regulation
- Team always has latest requirements
- No outdated frameworks

Synchronization:
Workflow changes â†’ References update automatically
```

**Link to Active Work:**

```
Task-to-Requirement Linkage:

Reference: "A.9.4.3: Multi-Factor Authentication"
     â†“ (linked to)
Tasks:
â”œâ”€ "Research MFA solutions"
â”œâ”€ "Purchase MFA licenses"
â””â”€ "Deploy MFA"

Benefits:
- Track which requirements are covered
- Identify gaps (requirements with no tasks)
- Audit trail (show how requirement was met)
- Coverage reporting (% of requirements addressed)
```

**Use Case Example:**

```
Compliance Board Setup:

Step 1: Export ISO 27001 workflow to board
Result: 93 controls appear in References column

Step 2: Client creates implementation tasks in To Do
Result: Execution tasks in main columns

Step 3: Link tasks to requirements
Task "Implement MFA" linked to Control "A.9.4.3"

Step 4: Auditor visits
Shows:
- Control A.9.4.3 in References (requirement)
- Linked tasks showing implementation (evidence)
- Clear traceability
- Audit success

References column = Compliance backbone of board
```

---

## CHAPTER 5: MANAGING CARDS (TASKS)

Cards are the fundamental unit of work on a board, representing individual tasks, deliverables, or action items.

### 5.1 Creating Cards

**Two Creation Methods:**

**Quick Create - Fast Entry:**

```
Purpose: Rapid task capture

Location: Each column has [+ Add Card] button

Click [+ Add Card]:
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ [Task title_______________] â”‚ â† Type title
â”‚ [Add Card]                  â”‚ â† Press Enter or click
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

Workflow:
1. Click [+ Add Card] in desired column
2. Type task title
3. Press Enter (or click Add Card)
4. Card appears at bottom of column
5. Ready for next task

Ideal for:
- Brainstorming sessions
- Sprint planning
- Rapid task entry
- Initial task capture
```

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
```

### 5.3 Moving Cards

**Drag and Drop - Primary Method:**

**How to Drag:**

```
1. Click and Hold Card
   - Mouse down on card
   - Hold for ~200ms
   - Card "lifts" (shadow appears)

2. Drag to Target Column
   - Move mouse while holding
   - Card follows cursor
   - Target column highlights

3. Drop to Release
   - Release mouse button
   - Card settles into column
   - Animation completes

4. Visual Feedback During Drag
   - Card has elevation/shadow
   - Target column glows or changes color
   - Drop zones indicated
   - Invalid drop zones marked (locked columns)
```

**Drag Example:**

```
Before:
[To Do]        [In Progress]    [Done]
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”   â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”    â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ Task A   â”‚   â”‚ Task C   â”‚    â”‚ Task E   â”‚
â”‚ Task B   â”‚   â”‚ Task D   â”‚    â”‚ Task F   â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜   â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜    â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

Drag "Task A" to "In Progress":

During Drag:
[To Do]        [In Progress]    [Done]
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”   â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”    â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ Task B   â”‚   â”‚â–“â–“â–“â–“â–“â–“â–“â–“â–“â–“â”‚    â”‚ Task E   â”‚
â”‚          â”‚   â”‚ Task C   â”‚    â”‚ Task F   â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜   â”‚ Task D   â”‚    â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
  Task A â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€>â”‚ Drop Hereâ”‚

                â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

**Locked Columns Reject Drops:**

```
Attempting to drag OUT of References column:

[References]   [To Do]
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”   â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”

  Req A â”€â”€â”€â”€âœ—â”€â”€â”€â”€> [To Do]
                      â†‘
              (Rejects drop)

- Cursor shows "not allowed" icon (ğŸš«)
- Column doesn't highlight
- Card snaps back to original position

"Cannot move cards out of locked References column"
```

**Reordering Within Column:**

```
Drag within same column to reorder:

Before:
[To Do]
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ Task A   â”‚
â”‚ Task B   â”‚
â”‚ Task C   â”‚
```

### 5.5 Card Properties

Detailed explanation of each card property.

**Title (Required):**

```
Purpose: Main task identifier

Field: [Draft Multi-Factor Authentication Policy__]

Requirements:
- Required (cannot be empty)
- 1-200 characters
- Plain text only

Edit:
- Click to edit inline in modal
- Type new title
- Press Enter or click away
- Auto-saves on blur

Best Practices:
âœ“ Start with verb ("Draft", "Configure", "Review")
âœ“ Be specific and clear
âœ“ Include what and optionally who/when
âœ“ Keep concise but meaningful

Examples:
âœ“ "Draft MFA Policy"
âœ“ "Configure Azure AD SSO"
âœ“ "Review Q1 Security Metrics"
âœ“ "Complete GDPR Training (All Staff)"

Avoid:
âœ— "Do this"
âœ— "Task"
âœ— "Follow up"
```

---

**Description:**

```
Purpose: Detailed task information

Field: Rich text editor
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ **What:** Create comprehensive MFA  â”‚
â”‚ policy                              â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚ **Why:** Required for ISO 27001     â”‚
â”‚ control A.9.4.3                     â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚ **How:**                            â”‚
â”‚ 1. Review existing policies         â”‚
â”‚ 2. Draft new sections               â”‚
â”‚ 3. Get legal review                 â”‚
â”‚ 4. Publish to intranet              â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚ **Success Criteria:**               â”‚
â”‚ - All scenarios covered             â”‚
â”‚ - Legal approved                    â”‚
â”‚ - Published and communicated        â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

Rich Text Support:
- Bold, italic, underline
- Bullet lists, numbered lists
- Links
- Headings
- Formatted content

What to Include:
- What needs to be done
- Why it's important
- How to do it (steps)
- Success criteria
- Constraints or dependencies
```

---

**Column:**

```
Purpose: Current workflow state

Field: [In Progress â–¼] (dropdown)

Options: All board columns
- To Do
- In Progress
- Review
- Done
- (Custom columns)

Alternative to Drag-Drop:
- Open card modal
- Change column dropdown
- Card moves immediately
- Same result as dragging

Use When:
- Card modal already open
- Prefer keyboard navigation
- Drag-drop not available (mobile)
```

---

**Done Status:**

```
Purpose: Mark task completion

Field: â˜ Done (checkbox)

States:
â˜ Not done (unchecked)
â˜‘ Done (checked)

Independent of Column:
- Can mark done in any column
- Done status â‰  column location

Example:
Task in "Review" column can be:
- Not done (awaiting review)
- Done (review complete, just not moved to Done column yet)

Used For:
- Milestone progress calculation
- Progress tracking
- Filtering done tasks
- Visual indicator on card face

Best Practice:
Mark done when work is truly complete and accepted
```

---

**Category:**

```
Purpose: Organizational grouping by type/theme

Field: [Documentation â–¼] (dropdown)

Single Category Assignment:
- One category per card
- Choose from board categories
- Or select "None"

Visual Badge:
- Shows on card face
- Category color and icon
- Quick identification

Example Categories:
ğŸ“„ Documentation
ğŸ’» Technical
ğŸ‘¥ HR
ğŸ”§ Configuration
ğŸ“Š Reporting
ğŸ”’ Security

Use Cases:
- Department-specific views (filter by HR)
- Task type (Documentation vs Technical)
- Priority (Urgent vs Routine)
- Workflow stage (Planning vs Execution)
```

---

**Milestone:**

```
Purpose: Link to time-based or goal-based phase

Field: [Sprint 1 â–¼] (dropdown)

Options:
- All board milestones
- None (unlink)

Progress Tracking:
- Milestone calculates progress from linked cards
- Mark card done â†’ Milestone progress increases

Visual Badge:
- Shows on card face
- Milestone name
- ğŸ¯ icon

Example:
Card: "Draft MFA Policy"
Milestone: "Sprint 1"

Sprint 1 progress:
- 20 cards linked
- 12 cards done
- 60% complete

This card contributes to that 60%

Filter by Milestone:
Click milestone badge â†’ Board filters to show only Sprint 1 cards
```

```
Purpose: Deadline tracking
```

---

**Effort:**

```
Purpose: Time tracking and capacity planning

Fields:
- Estimated: [8____] hours
- Actual: [6____] hours (optional)

Numeric Input:
- Enter hours as number
- Decimal allowed (e.g., 2.5 hours)
- Optional field

Displays on Card Face:
â±ï¸ 8h est
Or:
â±ï¸ 8h / 6h act

Use Cases:
- Sprint planning (total estimated hours vs team capacity)
- Time tracking (actual vs estimated)
- Workload distribution
- Project estimation

Example:
Sprint 1 capacity: 120 hours
Total estimated effort: 95 hours
Remaining capacity: 25 hours

Can add 3 more small tasks (8h each)
```

---

**Assignments:**

```
Purpose: Team collaboration and role clarity

Multiple People:
- Can assign multiple members
- Each with specific role
- All see task in "My Tasks" view

Four Roles:

1. Executor ğŸ› ï¸
   - Does the work
   - Primary responsible party
   - "Owner" of task

2. Approver âœ…
   - Reviews and approves
   - Quality gate
   - Final say on completion

3. Follower ğŸ‘ï¸
   - Stays informed
   - Receives notifications
   - Not actively involved
   - Interested party

4. Supervisor ğŸ‘”
   - Oversees work
   - Provides guidance
   - Escalation point
   - Management oversight

Assignment Example:
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ Assignments:                        â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚ ğŸ‘¤ Sarah Johnson (Executor) ğŸ› ï¸     â”‚
â”‚ ğŸ‘¤ Mike Chen (Approver) âœ…          â”‚
â”‚ ğŸ‘¤ Lisa Park (Follower) ğŸ‘ï¸         â”‚
â”‚ ğŸ‘¤ John Smith (Supervisor) ğŸ‘”       â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚ [+ Add Assignment]                  â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

Avatar Display:
Card face shows assignee avatars

- Clear responsibilities
- No confusion on who does what
- Proper oversight
- Informed stakeholders
```

---

**Groups:**

```
Purpose: Cross-cutting organization, bulk operations

Multiple Group Membership:
- Card can belong to multiple groups
- Checkbox selection
- Not exclusive (unlike category)

Selection:
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ Groups:                             â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚ â˜‘ MFA Implementation               â”‚
â”‚ â˜ Encryption Project               â”‚
â”‚ â˜‘ Q1 Initiatives                   â”‚
â”‚ â˜ Technical Debt                   â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

Check boxes for groups this card belongs to

Cross-Cutting Organization:
- One card in multiple groups
- Flexible categorization
- Multi-dimensional organization

Example:
Card: "Configure MFA in Azure AD"
Groups:
- MFA Implementation (project group)
- Q1 Initiatives (timeline group)
- Azure Changes (technical group)

Belongs to all three

Bulk Operation Targets:
Select group â†’ Perform action on all cards in group:
- Change milestone
- Change category
- Add label
- Bulk update

Group Progress:
Group card shows progress across all member cards
Useful for sub-project tracking
```

### 5.6 Deleting Cards

**When to Delete:**

```
Delete cards when:
âœ“ Task no longer needed
âœ“ Duplicate created by mistake
âœ“ Requirements changed
âœ“ Task obsolete

Don't delete:
âœ— Completed tasks (keep for history)
âœ— Tasks just "on hold" (mark as such instead)
```

**Delete Button in Modal:**

```
Location: Bottom of card details modal

[Delete Task] button (red)

Click to delete:
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  Delete Task?                    [Ã—]â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚  Delete "Draft MFA Policy"?         â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚  âš ï¸ This action cannot be undone    â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚  This will permanently delete:      â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Task details                     â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ All comments (3)                 â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ All attachments (5)              â”‚
â”‚  â€¢ Activity history                 â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚  Linked references will be unlinkedâ”‚
â”‚  Milestone/group membership removed â”‚
â”‚                                     â”‚
â”‚       [Cancel]  [Delete Forever]    â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

**Confirmation Required:**

```
Safety Measures:
- Must click through confirmation
- Shows what will be deleted
- Counts comments/attachments
- Warns about permanence
- Admin permission may be required

Prevents accidental deletion
```

**Permanent Removal:**

```
After deletion:
âœ— Card removed from board
âœ— All comments deleted
âœ— All attachments deleted
âœ— Activity history deleted
âœ— Cannot be undone or recovered

âœ“ Milestone/group/category unaffected (other cards remain)
âœ“ Linked references remain (just unlinked from this card)

Alternative to Deletion:
- Archive card (if feature available)
- Move to "Cancelled" or "Archived" column
- Mark with "Obsolete" label
- Keep history while removing from active view
```

---

**Plain Text:**

```
Format:
- Plain text only
- No rich formatting
- No bold, italic, etc.
- URLs auto-linked

Example:
See policy at https://company.com/policies/mfa
         â†‘
    (Automatically becomes clickable link)

Keep simple and fast
```

**Discussion Threads:**

```
Use comments for:
âœ“ Questions and answers
âœ“ Status updates
âœ“ Blockers and issues
âœ“ Coordination
âœ“ @ mentions for notifications

Example Thread:
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ Sarah: "Need legal approval"        â”‚
â”‚   â†“                                 â”‚
â”‚ Mike: "@John can you review?"       â”‚
â”‚   â†“                                 â”‚
â”‚ John: "Approved! Looks good"        â”‚
â”‚   â†“                                 â”‚
â”‚ Sarah: "Thanks! Publishing now"     â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

Conversation history preserved
```

**Newest First:**

```
Comment order:
- Most recent at top
- Oldest at bottom
- Scroll down for history
- Easy to see latest updates

Rationale:
Users care most about recent activity
Don't need to scroll to see latest
```

**Edit and Delete Own:**

```
Your own comments:
[Edit] [Delete] buttons visible

Others' comments:
No edit/delete buttons (read-only)

Edit:
- Click [Edit]
- Modify text
- Press Enter to save
- Or Cancel to discard

Delete:
- Click [Delete]
- Confirmation prompt
- Permanent removal
- Others still see "Comment deleted"
```

**Count Shown on Card Face:**

```
Card Display:
ğŸ’¬ 3

Indicates 3 comments on this task

Updates in real-time:
- Add comment â†’ count increases
- Delete comment â†’ count decreases

Visual indicator of discussion activity
```

## CHAPTER 7: MILESTONES

Organize tasks into time-based or goal-based phases for better tracking and reporting.

### 7.1 Understanding Milestones

**What are Milestones:**

Milestones are containers that group related cards together and automatically track their collective progress.

**Time-Based or Goal-Based Phases:**

```
Time-Based Examples:
â”œâ”€ Sprint 1 (2 weeks, Jan 1-14)
â”œâ”€ Sprint 2 (2 weeks, Jan 15-28)
â”œâ”€ Q1 2024 (3 months, Jan-Mar)
â””â”€ Phase 1: Discovery (1 month)

Goal-Based Examples:
â”œâ”€ ISO 27001 Certification
â”œâ”€ Product Launch v2.0
â”œâ”€ Security Improvements
â””â”€ Technical Debt Cleanup

Flexible:
- Define by timeframe
- Define by objective
- Hybrid (timeframe AND objective)
```

**Link Multiple Cards:**

```
One milestone â†’ Many cards

Example:
Milestone: "Sprint 1"
Linked Cards:
â”œâ”€ "Draft MFA policy" (To Do)
â”œâ”€ "Configure Azure AD" (In Progress)
â”œâ”€ "Test MFA" (In Progress)
â”œâ”€ "Deploy MFA" (Review)
â””â”€ "Train users" (Done)

5 cards linked to one milestone
```

**Auto-Track Progress:**

```
No manual updates needed!

Progress calculates automatically:
- 1 of 5 cards done = 20%
- 2 of 5 cards done = 40%
- 5 of 5 cards done = 100% (Completed)

Real-time:
- Mark card done â†’ Progress increases
- Unmark card â†’ Progress decreases

Always accurate
```

**Visual Organization:**

```
Milestone Carousel (top of board):

[Sprint 1 | Sprint 2 | Sprint 3 | Q1 Goals]
   60%        20%        0%         45%
    â†‘
Click to filter board

Filter Active:
Board shows only Sprint 1 cards
Other cards hidden
Clear filter to see all

Visual focus on current milestone
```

**Examples:**

```
Software Development:
â”œâ”€ Sprint 1, Sprint 2, Sprint 3...
â”œâ”€ Alpha Release, Beta Release, GA
â””â”€ Q1 Goals, Q2 Goals, Q3 Goals

Compliance:
â”œâ”€ ISO 27001 Certification
â”œâ”€ GDPR Implementation
â”œâ”€ SOC 2 Type 2 Audit
â””â”€ Annual Compliance Review

Project Management:
â”œâ”€ Discovery Phase
â”œâ”€ Design Phase
â”œâ”€ Implementation Phase
â”œâ”€ Testing Phase
â””â”€ Launch Phase

Manufacturing:
â”œâ”€ Prototype Build
â”œâ”€ Production Setup
â”œâ”€ Quality Testing
â””â”€ Market Launch
```

**Name (Required):**

```
Best Practices:
âœ“ Clear and concise
âœ“ Include timeframe or goal
âœ“ Meaningful to team

Examples:
âœ“ "Sprint 1 (Jan 1-14)"
âœ“ "Q1 2024 Compliance"
âœ“ "ISO 27001 Certification"
âœ“ "Product Launch v2.0"

Avoid:
âœ— "Milestone 1" (too vague)
âœ— "Tasks" (not descriptive)
âœ— "M1" (unclear abbreviation)
```

**Description (Optional):**

```
What to include:
- Milestone objective
- Timeframe (if not in name)
- Key deliverables
- Success criteria

Example:
"Two-week sprint focused on implementing MFA 
across all user authentication points. Includes 
Azure AD configuration, testing with pilot group, 
and initial rollout to IT department."

Provides context for team members
```

**Color Picker:**

```
Choose color for visual distinction:
ğŸ”µ Blue (default)
ğŸŸ¢ Green
ğŸŸ¡ Yellow
ğŸ”´ Red
ğŸŸ£ Purple
ğŸŸ¤ Brown

Use color strategically:
- Blue: Regular sprints
- Green: Completed milestones
- Yellow: In progress, attention needed
- Red: Urgent/critical milestones
- Purple: Special projects

Helps quick visual identification
```

**Creates Immediately:**

```
Click [Create Milestone]:
- Milestone created
- Appears in carousel
- Progress: 0% (no cards linked yet)
- Status: In Progress
- Ready to link cards

No separate save step
Instant availability
```

### 7.3 Milestone Properties

**Editable Properties:**

**Name (Editable):**

```
Change milestone name:
1. Click milestone card in carousel
2. Milestone details modal opens
3. Click [Edit] button
4. Update name
5. Click [Save]

Or:

Right-click milestone â†’ Rename
```

**Description (Editable):**

```
Update description:
- Same process as name edit
- Modify in milestone details modal
- Saves immediately
```

**Color (Editable):**

```
Change color:
- Milestone details modal
- Click color picker
- Select new color
- Milestone badge updates

Use case:
Change from Blue to Green when milestone 100% complete
Visual celebration of achievement
```

**Linked Cards (Auto-Count):**

```
Displays automatically:

Milestone Card:
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  Sprint 1      â”‚
â”‚  â–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–‘â–‘â–‘â–‘ 60%â”‚
â”‚  12 / 20 cards â”‚ â† Auto-count
â”‚  Due: Jan 15   â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

12 cards done / 20 total cards linked

Real-time updates:
- Link card â†’ Total increases
- Unlink card â†’ Total decreases
- No manual counting needed
```

**Progress (Auto-Calculated):**

```
Formula:
Progress = (Done cards / Total linked cards) Ã— 100%

Example:
Sprint 1:
- 20 cards linked
- 12 cards marked done
- Progress: 12/20 = 60%

Display: â–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–‘â–‘â–‘â–‘ 60%

Automatic calculation
Always accurate
```

**Status: In Progress or Completed:**

```
Two status states:

In Progress (Blue):
- Some cards not done
- Progress < 100%
- Ongoing work

Completed (Green):
- ALL cards done
- Progress = 100%
- Milestone achieved

Status auto-updates:
- Last card marked done â†’ Status: Completed
- Any card unmarked â†’ Status: In Progress

No manual status management needed
```

---

### 7.4 Status Calculation

**Completed Status:**

**ALL Linked Cards Marked Done:**

```
Requirement:
Every single linked card must be checked â˜‘ Done

Example:
Milestone: "Sprint 1"
Linked cards:
â˜‘ Task 1 (Done)
â˜‘ Task 2 (Done)
â˜‘ Task 3 (Done)
â˜‘ Task 4 (Done)
â˜‘ Task 5 (Done)

All 5 done â†’ Status: Completed
```

**Green Indicator:**

```
Completed Milestone Display:

â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ âœ“ Sprint 1     â”‚ â† Green checkmark
â”‚ â–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆ 100%â”‚ â† Full green progress bar
â”‚ 5 / 5 cards    â”‚
â”‚ Completed!     â”‚ â† Status text
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

```

**100% Progress:**

```
Progress bar filled:
â–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆ 100%

All tasks accomplished
Milestone objective achieved
```

---

**In Progress Status:**

**ANY Linked Card Not Done:**

```
Requirement:
At least one card is unchecked â˜ Not done

Example:
Milestone: "Sprint 1"
Linked cards:
â˜‘ Task 1 (Done)
â˜‘ Task 2 (Done)
â˜‘ Task 3 (Done)
â˜ Task 4 (Not done)
â˜ Task 5 (Not done)

2 not done â†’ Status: In Progress
```

**Blue Indicator:**

```
In Progress Milestone Display:

â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚  Sprint 1      â”‚ â† Blue (default)
â”‚  â–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–ˆâ–‘â–‘â–‘â–‘ 60%â”‚ â† Partial progress bar
â”‚  3 / 5 cards   â”‚
â”‚  In Progress   â”‚ â† Status text
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜

Work ongoing
Partial completion visible
```

**Percentage Shown (e.g., "3/5"):**

```
Format: Done / Total

Examples:
3 / 5 cards (60%)
12 / 20 cards (60%)
1 / 10 cards (10%)
9 / 10 cards (90%)

Numerator: Done count
Denominator: Total count
Percentage: Calculated and displayed
```

```
1. Open card details modal
2. Click milestone dropdown
3. Select "None"
4. Card unlinks
5. Milestone progress updates (card removed from count)

Card no longer associated with any milestone
```
